The minimalist interface hides a number of powerful writing features\r\n\r\nWORDCOUNT TOOLS\r\n===============\r\nSee at a glance how many words are in your document, or how many you've written since you opened the app. \r\n\r\nWORDCOUNT GOAL\r\n==============\r\nSet yourself a target - for example, 500 words - and Poe will let you know when you've reached that goal with a non-intrusive toast notification\r\n\r\nWRITING TIMER\r\n=============\r\nGot a limited amount of time to write?
